posted:Posted May 9, 2024
msg:The price/performance ratio of the room rate during the May Day holiday is still good, and the increase is not much compared with other hotels. The room I booked is 1 big bed + 1 small bed. The bed is quite big and the mattress is soft. Overall, it is good. Convenient to travel. During the long holiday, foreign tourists can take the bus line for free with their ID cards. There are many bus stops around the hotel, which are well connected. It is not far from the West Gate and South Gate of Slender West Lake. Adults can walk around and get there. Sometimes it feels faster than a traffic jam. The hotel is considered an old five-star hotel. The lobby entrance is not on the main road, so it is easy to miss at first. When checking in, because the room was not ready, I waited for a while and gave a drink coupon for the coffee shop. Take the elevator with the room card. The room is quite large, with a bathtub and shower, which is quite convenient. Stayed for 2 nights and gave 2 servings of fruit, which is quite rare. Generally, hotels give fruit on the first day. Seeing that we took a bath, they also gave us a disposable bath bag, which is very considerate. Overall, the high-quality service made up for some shortcomings in the hardware, and the experience during the stay was still good.
